\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a522e6806948369987639a0d1df03c029}\label{namespaceoboe_a522e6806948369987639a0d1df03c029}} 
\index{oboe@{oboe}!ChannelCount@{ChannelCount}}
\index{ChannelCount@{ChannelCount}!oboe@{oboe}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ChannelCount}{ChannelCount}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a522e6806948369987639a0d1df03c029}{oboe\+::\+Channel\+Count}} \+: int32\+\_\+t}

The channel count of the audio stream. The underlying type is {\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t}. Use of this enum is convenient to avoid \char`\"{}magic\char`\"{} numbers when specifying the channel count.

For example, you can write {\ttfamily builder.\+set\+Channel\+Count(\+Channel\+Count\+::\+Stereo)} rather than {\ttfamily builder.\+set\+Channel\+Count(2)} \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Unspecified@{Unspecified}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Unspecified@{Unspecified}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a522e6806948369987639a0d1df03c029ae9d0f75ff535830d677bf32c19bfe3be}\label{namespaceoboe_a522e6806948369987639a0d1df03c029ae9d0f75ff535830d677bf32c19bfe3be}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a522e6806948369987639a0d1df03c029}\label{namespaceoboe_a522e6806948369987639a0d1df03c029}} 
\index{oboe@{oboe}!ChannelCount@{ChannelCount}}
\index{ChannelCount@{ChannelCount}!oboe@{oboe}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ChannelCount}{ChannelCount}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a522e6806948369987639a0d1df03c029}{oboe\+::\+Channel\+Count}} \+: int32\+\_\+t}

The channel count of the audio stream. The underlying type is {\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t}. Use of this enum is convenient to avoid \char`\"{}magic\char`\"{} numbers when specifying the channel count.

For example, you can write {\ttfamily builder.\+set\+Channel\+Count(\+Channel\+Count\+::\+Stereo)} rather than {\ttfamily builder.\+set\+Channel\+Count(2)} \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a522e6806948369987639a0d1df03c029}\label{namespaceoboe_a522e6806948369987639a0d1df03c029}} 
\index{oboe@{oboe}!ChannelCount@{ChannelCount}}
\index{ChannelCount@{ChannelCount}!oboe@{oboe}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ChannelCount}{ChannelCount}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a522e6806948369987639a0d1df03c029}{oboe\+::\+Channel\+Count}} \+: int32\+\_\+t}

The channel count of the audio stream. The underlying type is {\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t}. Use of this enum is convenient to avoid \char`\"{}magic\char`\"{} numbers when specifying the channel count.

For example, you can write {\ttfamily builder.\+set\+Channel\+Count(\+Channel\+Count\+::\+Stereo)} rather than {\ttfamily builder.\+set\+Channel\+Count(2)} \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a522e6806948369987639a0d1df03c029}\label{namespaceoboe_a522e6806948369987639a0d1df03c029}} 
\index{oboe@{oboe}!ChannelCount@{ChannelCount}}
\index{ChannelCount@{ChannelCount}!oboe@{oboe}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ChannelCount}{ChannelCount}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a522e6806948369987639a0d1df03c029}{oboe\+::\+Channel\+Count}} \+: int32\+\_\+t}

The channel count of the audio stream. The underlying type is {\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t}. Use of this enum is convenient to avoid \char`\"{}magic\char`\"{} numbers when specifying the channel count.

For example, you can write {\ttfamily builder.\+set\+Channel\+Count(\+Channel\+Count\+::\+Stereo)} rather than {\ttfamily builder.\+set\+Channel\+Count(2)} \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Unspecified@{Unspecified}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Unspecified@{Unspecified}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a522e6806948369987639a0d1df03c029ae9d0f75ff535830d677bf32c19bfe3be}\label{namespaceoboe_a522e6806948369987639a0d1df03c029ae9d0f75ff535830d677bf32c19bfe3be}}

\index{oboe@{oboe}!ContentType@{ContentType}}
\index{ContentType@{ContentType}!oboe@{oboe}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ContentType}{ContentType}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a2a3cec6f021c1a324df60273710c604b}{oboe\+::\+Content\+Type}} \+: int32\+\_\+t}

The Content\+Type attribute describes {\itshape what} you are playing. It expresses the general category of the content. This information is optional. But in case it is known (for instance \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a2a3cec6f021c1a324df60273710c604ba0226bd14541ccf7d03832fc2a3b3f694}{Movie}} for a movie streaming service or \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a2a3cec6f021c1a324df60273710c604bad9d5b99135c2c0507902d47d73ff9f60}{Speech}} for an audio book application) this information might be used by the audio framework to enforce audio focus.

Note that these match the equivalent values in Audio\+Attributes in the Android Java A\+PI.

This attribute only has an effect on Android A\+PI 28+. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Speech@{Speech}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Speech@{Speech}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a2a3cec6f021c1a324df60273710c604bad9d5b99135c2c0507902d47d73ff9f60}\label{namespaceoboe_a2a3cec6f021c1a324df60273710c604bad9d5b99135c2c0507902d47d73ff9f60}} 
Speech&Use this for spoken voice, audio books, etcetera. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Music@{Music}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Music@{Music}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a2a3cec6f021c1a324df60273710c604bac7cae0c44fae54877dacd14eea956add}\label{namespaceoboe_a2a3cec6f021c1a324df60273710c604bac7cae0c44fae54877dacd14eea956add}}

Movie&Use this for a movie or video soundtrack. \\

\index{oboe@{oboe}!ContentType@{ContentType}}
\index{ContentType@{ContentType}!oboe@{oboe}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ContentType}{ContentType}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a2a3cec6f021c1a324df60273710c604b}{oboe\+::\+Content\+Type}} \+: int32\+\_\+t}

The Content\+Type attribute describes {\itshape what} you are playing. It expresses the general category of the content. This information is optional. But in case it is known (for instance \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a2a3cec6f021c1a324df60273710c604ba0226bd14541ccf7d03832fc2a3b3f694}{Movie}} for a movie streaming service or \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a2a3cec6f021c1a324df60273710c604bad9d5b99135c2c0507902d47d73ff9f60}{Speech}} for an audio book application) this information might be used by the audio framework to enforce audio focus.

Note that these match the equivalent values in Audio\+Attributes in the Android Java A\+PI.

This attribute only has an effect on Android A\+PI 28+. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Speech@{Speech}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Speech@{Speech}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a2a3cec6f021c1a324df60273710c604bad9d5b99135c2c0507902d47d73ff9f60}\label{namespaceoboe_a2a3cec6f021c1a324df60273710c604bad9d5b99135c2c0507902d47d73ff9f60}} 
Speech&Use this for spoken voice, audio books, etcetera. \\
\hline

\index{oboe@{oboe}!InputPreset@{InputPreset}}
\index{InputPreset@{InputPreset}!oboe@{oboe}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{InputPreset}{InputPreset}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06}{oboe\+::\+Input\+Preset}} \+: int32\+\_\+t}

Defines the audio source. An audio source defines both a default physical source of audio signal, and a recording configuration.

Note that these match the equivalent values in Media\+Recorder.\+Audio\+Source in the Android Java A\+PI.

This attribute only has an effect on Android A\+PI 28+. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Generic@{Generic}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Generic@{Generic}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06af04821446490aa85b8b7622ae067dc68}\label{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06af04821446490aa85b8b7622ae067dc68}} 
Generic&Use this preset when other presets do not apply. \\
\hline

Camcorder&Use this preset when recording video. \\

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06}\label{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06}} 
\index{oboe@{oboe}!InputPreset@{InputPreset}}
\index{InputPreset@{InputPreset}!oboe@{oboe}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{InputPreset}{InputPreset}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06}{oboe\+::\+Input\+Preset}} \+: int32\+\_\+t}

Defines the audio source. An audio source defines both a default physical source of audio signal, and a recording configuration.

Note that these match the equivalent values in Media\+Recorder.\+Audio\+Source in the Android Java A\+PI.

This attribute only has an effect on Android A\+PI 28+. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Generic@{Generic}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Generic@{Generic}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06af04821446490aa85b8b7622ae067dc68}\label{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06af04821446490aa85b8b7622ae067dc68}} 
Generic&Use this preset when other presets do not apply. \\
\hline

Camcorder&Use this preset when recording video. \\

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06}\label{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06}} 
\index{oboe@{oboe}!InputPreset@{InputPreset}}
\index{InputPreset@{InputPreset}!oboe@{oboe}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{InputPreset}{InputPreset}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06}{oboe\+::\+Input\+Preset}} \+: int32\+\_\+t}

Defines the audio source. An audio source defines both a default physical source of audio signal, and a recording configuration.

Note that these match the equivalent values in Media\+Recorder.\+Audio\+Source in the Android Java A\+PI.

This attribute only has an effect on Android A\+PI 28+. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Generic@{Generic}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Generic@{Generic}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06af04821446490aa85b8b7622ae067dc68}\label{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06af04821446490aa85b8b7622ae067dc68}} 
Generic&Use this preset when other presets do not apply. \\
\hline

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06}\label{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06}} 
\index{oboe@{oboe}!InputPreset@{InputPreset}}
\index{InputPreset@{InputPreset}!oboe@{oboe}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{InputPreset}{InputPreset}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06}{oboe\+::\+Input\+Preset}} \+: int32\+\_\+t}

Defines the audio source. An audio source defines both a default physical source of audio signal, and a recording configuration.

Note that these match the equivalent values in Media\+Recorder.\+Audio\+Source in the Android Java A\+PI.

This attribute only has an effect on Android A\+PI 28+. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Generic@{Generic}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Generic@{Generic}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06af04821446490aa85b8b7622ae067dc68}\label{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06af04821446490aa85b8b7622ae067dc68}} 
Generic&Use this preset when other presets do not apply. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Unprocessed@{Unprocessed}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Unprocessed@{Unprocessed}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06a2e5674c6a486085a7451e886a3b52c64}\label{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06a2e5674c6a486085a7451e886a3b52c64}} 
Unprocessed&Use this preset to obtain an input with no effects. Note that this input will not have automatic gain control so the recorded volume may be very low. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{VoicePerformance@{VoicePerformance}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!VoicePerformance@{VoicePerformance}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06aaa0da699e26bca612352f51be4790fe0}\label{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06aaa0da699e26bca612352f51be4790fe0}} 
Voice\+Performance&Use this preset for capturing audio meant to be processed in real time and played back for live performance (e.\+g karaoke). The capture path will minimize latency and coupling with playback path. \\

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SessionId}{SessionId}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a5752250c10e96179e3618d7f72937eaf}{oboe\+::\+Session\+Id}}}

This attribute can be used to allocate a session ID to the audio stream.

This attribute only has an effect on Android A\+PI 28+. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}

Allocate&Allocate a session ID that can be used to attach and control effects using the Java Audio\+Effects A\+PI. Note that the use of this flag may result in higher latency.

Note that this matches the value of Audio\+Manager.\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+S\+E\+S\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+I\+D\+\_\+\+G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+TE. \\

{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a5752250c10e96179e3618d7f72937eaf}{oboe\+::\+Session\+Id}}}

This attribute can be used to allocate a session ID to the audio stream.

\index{oboe@{oboe}!SessionId@{SessionId}}
\index{SessionId@{SessionId}!oboe@{oboe}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SessionId}{SessionId}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a5752250c10e96179e3618d7f72937eaf}{oboe\+::\+Session\+Id}}}

This attribute can be used to allocate a session ID to the audio stream.

This attribute only has an effect on Android A\+PI 28+. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{None@{None}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!None@{None}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a5752250c10e96179e3618d7f72937eafa97d445b4d331dc28ce5c1db98c5cfa4f}\label{namespaceoboe_a5752250c10e96179e3618d7f72937eafa97d445b4d331dc28ce5c1db98c5cfa4f}} 
None&Do not allocate a session ID. Effects cannot be used with this stream. Default. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{None@{None}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!None@{None}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a5752250c10e96179e3618d7f72937eafa6adf97f83acf6453d4a6a4b1070f3754}\label{namespaceoboe_a5752250c10e96179e3618d7f72937eafa6adf97f83acf6453d4a6a4b1070f3754}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a8330247b25429953a08354f41834d520}{oboe\+::\+Sharing\+Mode}} \+: int32\+\_\+t\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}

The sharing mode of the audio stream. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Exclusive@{Exclusive}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Exclusive@{Exclusive}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a8330247b25429953a08354f41834d520a2ef50b4c466304dc6ac77bac8a779971}\label{namespaceoboe_a8330247b25429953a08354f41834d520a2ef50b4c466304dc6ac77bac8a779971}} 
Exclusive&This will be the only stream using a particular source or sink. This mode will provide the lowest possible latency. You should close E\+X\+C\+L\+U\+S\+I\+VE streams immediately when you are not using them.

If you do not need the lowest possible latency then we recommend using Shared, which is the default. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Shared@{Shared}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Shared@{Shared}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a8330247b25429953a08354f41834d520aa6156ea9d66fef24e87e841fbabf7cca}\label{namespaceoboe_a8330247b25429953a08354f41834d520aa6156ea9d66fef24e87e841fbabf7cca}} 
Shared&Multiple applications can share the same device. The data from output streams will be mixed by the audio service. The data for input streams will be distributed by the audio service.

This will have higher latency than the E\+X\+C\+L\+U\+S\+I\+VE mode. \\
\hline

Exclusive&This will be the only stream using a particular source or sink. This mode will provide the lowest possible latency. You should close E\+X\+C\+L\+U\+S\+I\+VE streams immediately when you are not using them.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Usage}{Usage}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0}{oboe\+::\+Usage}} \+: int32\+\_\+t\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}

The Usage attribute expresses {\itshape why} you are playing a sound, what is this sound used for. This information is used by certain platforms or routing policies to make more refined volume or routing decisions.

Note that these match the equivalent values in Audio\+Attributes in the Android Java A\+PI.

This attribute only has an effect on Android A\+PI 28+. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Media@{Media}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Media@{Media}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0a3b563524fdb17b4a86590470d40bef74}\label{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0a3b563524fdb17b4a86590470d40bef74}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0}\label{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0}} 
\index{oboe@{oboe}!Usage@{Usage}}
\index{Usage@{Usage}!oboe@{oboe}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Usage}{Usage}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0}{oboe\+::\+Usage}} \+: int32\+\_\+t\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}

The Usage attribute expresses {\itshape why} you are playing a sound, what is this sound used for. This information is used by certain platforms or routing policies to make more refined volume or routing decisions.

Note that these match the equivalent values in Audio\+Attributes in the Android Java A\+PI.

This attribute only has an effect on Android A\+PI 28+. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Media@{Media}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Media@{Media}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0a3b563524fdb17b4a86590470d40bef74}\label{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0a3b563524fdb17b4a86590470d40bef74}} 
Media&Use this for streaming media, music performance, video, podcasts, etcetera. \\
\hline

Voice\+Communication&Use this for voice over IP, telephony, etcetera. \\

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0}\label{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0}} 
\index{oboe@{oboe}!Usage@{Usage}}
\index{Usage@{Usage}!oboe@{oboe}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Usage}{Usage}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0}{oboe\+::\+Usage}} \+: int32\+\_\+t\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}

The Usage attribute expresses {\itshape why} you are playing a sound, what is this sound used for. This information is used by certain platforms or routing policies to make more refined volume or routing decisions.

Note that these match the equivalent values in Audio\+Attributes in the Android Java A\+PI.

This attribute only has an effect on Android A\+PI 28+. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Media@{Media}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Media@{Media}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0a3b563524fdb17b4a86590470d40bef74}\label{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0a3b563524fdb17b4a86590470d40bef74}} 
Media&Use this for streaming media, music performance, video, podcasts, etcetera. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{VoiceCommunication@{VoiceCommunication}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!VoiceCommunication@{VoiceCommunication}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06a5bad8854288c956062ec1d4d7c14fed6}\label{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06a5bad8854288c956062ec1d4d7c14fed6}} 
Voice\+Communication&Use this for voice over IP, telephony, etcetera. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{VoiceCommunicationSignalling@{VoiceCommunicationSignalling}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!VoiceCommunicationSignalling@{VoiceCommunicationSignalling}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0a404f62633744bf4da0c6a27a2b78ce74}\label{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0a404f62633744bf4da0c6a27a2b78ce74}}

Alarm&Use this to demand the users attention. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Notification@{Notification}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Notification@{Notification}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0a96d008db67fc0b5551a926842bbb6a71}\label{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0a96d008db67fc0b5551a926842bbb6a71}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0}\label{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0}} 
\index{oboe@{oboe}!Usage@{Usage}}
\index{Usage@{Usage}!oboe@{oboe}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Usage}{Usage}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0}{oboe\+::\+Usage}} \+: int32\+\_\+t\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}

The Usage attribute expresses {\itshape why} you are playing a sound, what is this sound used for. This information is used by certain platforms or routing policies to make more refined volume or routing decisions.

Note that these match the equivalent values in Audio\+Attributes in the Android Java A\+PI.

This attribute only has an effect on Android A\+PI 28+. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Media@{Media}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Media@{Media}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0a3b563524fdb17b4a86590470d40bef74}\label{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0a3b563524fdb17b4a86590470d40bef74}} 
Media&Use this for streaming media, music performance, video, podcasts, etcetera. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{VoiceCommunication@{VoiceCommunication}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!VoiceCommunication@{VoiceCommunication}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06a5bad8854288c956062ec1d4d7c14fed6}\label{namespaceoboe_a4477ed232b02e2694d9309baf55a8f06a5bad8854288c956062ec1d4d7c14fed6}} 
Voice\+Communication&Use this for voice over IP, telephony, etcetera. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{VoiceCommunicationSignalling@{VoiceCommunicationSignalling}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!VoiceCommunicationSignalling@{VoiceCommunicationSignalling}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0a404f62633744bf4da0c6a27a2b78ce74}\label{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0a404f62633744bf4da0c6a27a2b78ce74}} 
Voice\+Communication\+Signalling&Use this for sounds associated with telephony such as busy tones, D\+T\+MF, etcetera. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Alarm@{Alarm}!oboe@{oboe}}\index{oboe@{oboe}!Alarm@{Alarm}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0a46c4c4d980dfe025ae5b35aa0011dde4}\label{namespaceoboe_a104ee8396c173fefac429759ea3c21a0a46c4c4d980dfe025ae5b35aa0011dde4}}

\index{oboe@{oboe}!convertToText@{convertToText}}
\index{convertToText@{convertToText}!oboe@{oboe}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{convertToText()}{convertToText()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename From\+Type $>$ \\
const char $\ast$ oboe\+::convert\+To\+Text (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{From\+Type}]{input }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

The text is the A\+S\+C\+II symbol corresponding to the supplied Oboe enum value, or an English message saying the value is unrecognized. This is intended for developers to use when debugging. It is not for displaying to users.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em input} & object to convert from. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
common/\+Utilities.\+cpp for concrete implementations 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
text representation of an Oboe enum value. There is no need to call free on this. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{oboe@{oboe}!getSdkVersion@{getSdkVersion}}
\index{getSdkVersion@{getSdkVersion}!oboe@{oboe}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getSdkVersion()}{getSdkVersion()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int oboe\+::get\+Sdk\+Version (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Return the version of the S\+DK that is currently running.

For example, on Android, this would return 27 for Oreo 8.\+1. If the version number cannot be determined then this will return -\/1.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
version number or -\/1 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceoboe_a0319b95b18762637b6d0456a880e5fca}\label{namespaceoboe_a0319b95b18762637b6d0456a880e5fca}} 
\index{oboe@{oboe}!OpenSLES\_createExtendedFormat@{OpenSLES\_createExtendedFormat}}
\index{OpenSLES\_createExtendedFormat@{OpenSLES\_createExtendedFormat}!oboe@{oboe}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{OpenSLES\_createExtendedFormat()}{OpenSLES\_createExtendedFormat()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily S\+L\+Android\+Data\+Format\+\_\+\+P\+C\+M\+\_\+\+EX oboe\+::\+Open\+S\+L\+E\+S\+\_\+create\+Extended\+Format (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{S\+L\+Data\+Format\+\_\+\+P\+CM}]{format,  }\item[{S\+Luint32}]{representation }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates an extended P\+CM format from the supplied format and data representation. This method should only be called on Android devices with A\+PI level 21+. A\+PI 21 introduced the S\+L\+Android\+Data\+Format\+\_\+\+P\+C\+M\+\_\+\+EX object which allows audio samples to be represented using single precision floating-\/point.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em format} & \\
\hline
{\em representation} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the extended P\+CM format 
\end{DoxyReturn}
